\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00133}00133\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00134}00134\ \textcolor{comment}{Converts\ PNG\ data\ in\ memory\ to\ raw\ pixel\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00135}00135\ \textcolor{comment}{out:\ Output\ parameter.\ Pointer\ to\ buffer\ that\ will\ contain\ the\ raw\ pixel\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00136}00136\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ After\ decoding,\ its\ size\ is\ w\ *\ h\ *\ (bytes\ per\ pixel)\ bytes\ larger\ than}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00137}00137\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ initially.\ Bytes\ per\ pixel\ depends\ on\ colortype\ and\ bitdepth.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00653}00653\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ strict\ requirements\ for\ the\ allowed\ sbit\ values\ in\ combination\ with\ color\ modes.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00655}00655\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ color\ mode,\ even\ if\ the\ pixel\ data\ would\ in\ fact\ fit\ in\ a\ more\ efficient\ 8-\/bit\ mode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00656}00656\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00666}00666\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00667}00667\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ unknown\ chunks:\ chunks\ not\ known\ by\ LodePNG,\ passed\ on\ byte\ for\ byte.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00668}00668\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00669}00669\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ There\ are\ 3\ buffers,\ one\ for\ each\ position\ in\ the\ PNG\ where\ unknown\ chunks\ can\ appear.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00672}00672\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ 0:\ between\ IHDR\ and\ PLTE,\ 1:\ between\ PLTE\ and\ IDAT,\ 2:\ between\ IDAT\ and\ IEND.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00673}00673\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00674}00674\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ For\ encoding,\ do\ not\ store\ critical\ chunks\ or\ known\ chunks\ that\ are\ enabled\ with\ a\ "{}\_defined"{}\ flag}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00676}00676\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ (such\ as\ one\ with\ two\ IHDR\ chunks\ or\ the\ disallowed\ combination\ of\ sRGB\ with\ iCCP).\ But\ do\ use}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00678}00678\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ or\ any\ non-\/standard\ PNG\ chunk.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00922}00922\ \textcolor{comment}{In\ the\ PNG\ file\ format,\ chunks\ have\ the\ following\ format:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00923}00923\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/4\ bytes\ length:\ length\ of\ the\ data\ of\ the\ chunk\ in\ bytes\ (chunk\ itself\ is\ 12\ bytes\ longer)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00924}00924\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/4\ bytes\ chunk\ type\ (ASCII\ a-\/z,A-\/Z\ only,\ see\ below)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00925}00925\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/length\ bytes\ of\ data\ (may\ be\ 0\ bytes\ if\ length\ was\ 0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00926}00926\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/4\ bytes\ of\ CRC,\ computed\ on\ chunk\ name\ +\ data}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00928}00928\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ first\ chunk\ starts\ at\ the\ 8th\ byte\ of\ the\ PNG\ file,\ the\ entire\ rest\ of\ the\ file}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00932}00932\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/First\ byte:\ uppercase\ =\ critical,\ lowercase\ =\ ancillary}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00933}00933\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/Second\ byte:\ uppercase\ =\ public,\ lowercase\ =\ private}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00934}00934\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/Third\ byte:\ must\ be\ uppercase}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l00935}00935\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/Fourth\ byte:\ uppercase\ =\ unsafe\ to\ copy,\ lowercase\ =\ safe\ to\ copy}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01226}01226\ \textcolor{comment}{LodePNG\ is\ a\ PNG\ codec\ according\ to\ the\ Portable\ Network\ Graphics\ (PNG)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01227}01227\ \textcolor{comment}{Specification\ (Second\ Edition)\ -\/\ W3C\ Recommendation\ 10\ November\ 2003.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01253}01253\ \textcolor{comment}{simplicity,\ the\ following\ design\ choices\ were\ made:\ There\ are\ no\ dependencies}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01257}01257\ \textcolor{comment}{the\ colors\ of\ the\ raw\ image\ are\ always\ RGB\ or\ RGBA,\ no\ matter\ what\ color\ type}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01262}01262\ \textcolor{comment}{programs,\ ...\ It's\ less\ suitable\ for\ full\ fledged\ image\ editors,\ loading\ PNGs}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01323}01323\ \textcolor{comment}{ignore\ it,\ and\ the\ C\ code\ is\ made\ to\ compile\ both\ with\ strict\ ISO\ C90\ and\ C++.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01465}01465\ \textcolor{comment}{*)\ add\_id:\ add\ text\ chunk\ "{}Encoder:\ LodePNG\ <version>"{}\ to\ the\ image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01466}01466\ \textcolor{comment}{*)\ text\_compression:\ default\ 1.\ If\ 1,\ it'll\ store\ texts\ as\ zTXt\ instead\ of\ tEXt\ chunks.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01467}01467\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ zTXt\ chunks\ use\ zlib\ compression\ on\ the\ text.\ This\ gives\ a\ smaller\ result\ on}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01482}01482\ \textcolor{comment}{well,\ though.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01483}01483\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01484}01484\ \textcolor{comment}{To\ be\ able\ to\ do\ this,\ LodePNG\ does\ conversions\ from\ one\ color\ mode\ to\ another.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01485}01485\ \textcolor{comment}{It\ can\ convert\ from\ almost\ any\ color\ type\ to\ any\ other\ color\ type,\ except\ the}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01487}01487\ \textcolor{comment}{palette\ when\ the\ palette\ doesn't\ have\ a\ required\ color\ is\ not\ supported.\ This\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01488}01488\ \textcolor{comment}{not\ supported\ on\ purpose:\ this\ is\ information\ loss\ which\ requires\ a\ color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01489}01489\ \textcolor{comment}{reduction\ algorithm\ that\ is\ beyond\ the\ scope\ of\ a\ PNG\ encoder\ (yes,\ RGB\ to\ gray}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01490}01490\ \textcolor{comment}{is\ easy,\ but\ there\ are\ multiple\ ways\ if\ you\ want\ to\ give\ some\ channels\ more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01491}01491\ \textcolor{comment}{weight).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01492}01492\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01493}01493\ \textcolor{comment}{By\ default,\ when\ decoding,\ you\ get\ the\ raw\ image\ in\ 32-\/bit\ RGBA\ or\ 24-\/bit\ RGB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01494}01494\ \textcolor{comment}{color,\ no\ matter\ what\ color\ type\ the\ PNG\ has.\ And\ by\ default\ when\ encoding,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01495}01495\ \textcolor{comment}{LodePNG\ automatically\ picks\ the\ best\ color\ model\ for\ the\ output\ PNG,\ and\ expects}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01496}01496\ \textcolor{comment}{the\ input\ image\ to\ be\ 32-\/bit\ RGBA\ or\ 24-\/bit\ RGB.\ So,\ unless\ you\ want\ to\ control}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01497}01497\ \textcolor{comment}{the\ color\ format\ of\ the\ images\ yourself,\ you\ can\ skip\ this\ chapter.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01499}01499\ \textcolor{comment}{6.1.\ PNG\ color\ types}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01500}01500\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01501}01501\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01502}01502\ \textcolor{comment}{A\ PNG\ image\ can\ have\ many\ color\ types,\ ranging\ from\ 1-\/bit\ color\ to\ 64-\/bit\ color,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01503}01503\ \textcolor{comment}{as\ well\ as\ palettized\ color\ modes.\ After\ the\ zlib\ decompression\ and\ unfiltering}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01504}01504\ \textcolor{comment}{in\ the\ PNG\ image\ is\ done,\ the\ raw\ pixel\ data\ will\ have\ that\ color\ type\ and\ thus}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01505}01505\ \textcolor{comment}{a\ certain\ amount\ of\ bits\ per\ pixel.\ If\ you\ want\ the\ output\ raw\ image\ after}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01506}01506\ \textcolor{comment}{decoding\ to\ have\ another\ color\ type,\ a\ conversion\ is\ done\ by\ LodePNG.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01507}01507\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01508}01508\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ PNG\ specification\ gives\ the\ following\ color\ types:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01509}01509\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01510}01510\ \textcolor{comment}{0:\ grayscale,\ bit\ depths\ 1,\ 2,\ 4,\ 8,\ 16}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01511}01511\ \textcolor{comment}{2:\ RGB,\ bit\ depths\ 8\ and\ 16}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01512}01512\ \textcolor{comment}{3:\ palette,\ bit\ depths\ 1,\ 2,\ 4\ and\ 8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01513}01513\ \textcolor{comment}{4:\ grayscale\ with\ alpha,\ bit\ depths\ 8\ and\ 16}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01514}01514\ \textcolor{comment}{6:\ RGBA,\ bit\ depths\ 8\ and\ 16}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01515}01515\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01516}01516\ \textcolor{comment}{Bit\ depth\ is\ the\ amount\ of\ bits\ per\ pixel\ per\ color\ channel.\ So\ the\ total\ amount}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01517}01517\ \textcolor{comment}{of\ bits\ per\ pixel\ is:\ amount\ of\ channels\ *\ bitdepth.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01518}01518\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01519}01519\ \textcolor{comment}{6.2.\ color\ conversions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01520}01520\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01521}01521\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01522}01522\ \textcolor{comment}{As\ explained\ in\ the\ sections\ about\ the\ encoder\ and\ decoder,\ you\ can\ specify}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01523}01523\ \textcolor{comment}{color\ types\ and\ bit\ depths\ in\ info\_png\ and\ info\_raw\ to\ change\ the\ default}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01524}01524\ \textcolor{comment}{behaviour.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01525}01525\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01526}01526\ \textcolor{comment}{If,\ when\ decoding,\ you\ want\ the\ raw\ image\ to\ be\ something\ else\ than\ the\ default,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01527}01527\ \textcolor{comment}{you\ need\ to\ set\ the\ color\ type\ and\ bit\ depth\ you\ want\ in\ the\ LodePNGColorMode,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01528}01528\ \textcolor{comment}{or\ the\ parameters\ colortype\ and\ bitdepth\ of\ the\ simple\ decoding\ function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01529}01529\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01530}01530\ \textcolor{comment}{If,\ when\ encoding,\ you\ use\ another\ color\ type\ than\ the\ default\ in\ the\ raw\ input}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01531}01531\ \textcolor{comment}{image,\ you\ need\ to\ specify\ its\ color\ type\ and\ bit\ depth\ in\ the\ LodePNGColorMode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01532}01532\ \textcolor{comment}{of\ the\ raw\ image,\ or\ use\ the\ parameters\ colortype\ and\ bitdepth\ of\ the\ simple}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01533}01533\ \textcolor{comment}{encoding\ function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01534}01534\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01535}01535\ \textcolor{comment}{If,\ when\ encoding,\ you\ don't\ want\ LodePNG\ to\ choose\ the\ output\ PNG\ color\ type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01536}01536\ \textcolor{comment}{but\ control\ it\ yourself,\ you\ need\ to\ set\ auto\_convert\ in\ the\ encoder\ settings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01537}01537\ \textcolor{comment}{to\ false,\ and\ specify\ the\ color\ type\ you\ want\ in\ the\ LodePNGInfo\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01538}01538\ \textcolor{comment}{encoder\ (including\ palette:\ it\ can\ generate\ a\ palette\ if\ auto\_convert\ is\ true,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01539}01539\ \textcolor{comment}{otherwise\ not).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01540}01540\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01541}01541\ \textcolor{comment}{If\ the\ input\ and\ output\ color\ type\ differ\ (whether\ user\ chosen\ or\ auto\ chosen),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01542}01542\ \textcolor{comment}{LodePNG\ will\ do\ a\ color\ conversion,\ which\ follows\ the\ rules\ below,\ and\ may}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01543}01543\ \textcolor{comment}{sometimes\ result\ in\ an\ error.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01544}01544\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01545}01545\ \textcolor{comment}{To\ avoid\ some\ confusion:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01546}01546\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/the\ decoder\ converts\ from\ PNG\ to\ raw\ image}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01547}01547\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/the\ encoder\ converts\ from\ raw\ image\ to\ PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01548}01548\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/the\ colortype\ and\ bitdepth\ in\ LodePNGColorMode\ info\_raw,\ are\ those\ of\ the\ raw\ image}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01549}01549\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/the\ colortype\ and\ bitdepth\ in\ the\ color\ field\ of\ LodePNGInfo\ info\_png,\ are\ those\ of\ the\ PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01550}01550\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/when\ encoding,\ the\ color\ type\ in\ LodePNGInfo\ is\ ignored\ if\ auto\_convert}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01551}01551\ \textcolor{comment}{\ is\ enabled,\ it\ is\ automatically\ generated\ instead}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01552}01552\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/when\ decoding,\ the\ color\ type\ in\ LodePNGInfo\ is\ set\ by\ the\ decoder\ to\ that\ of\ the\ original}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01553}01553\ \textcolor{comment}{\ PNG\ image,\ but\ it\ can\ be\ ignored\ since\ the\ raw\ image\ has\ the\ color\ type\ you\ requested\ instead}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01554}01554\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/if\ the\ color\ type\ of\ the\ LodePNGColorMode\ and\ PNG\ image\ aren't\ the\ same,\ a\ conversion}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01555}01555\ \textcolor{comment}{\ between\ the\ color\ types\ is\ done\ if\ the\ color\ types\ are\ supported.\ If\ it\ is\ not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01556}01556\ \textcolor{comment}{\ supported,\ an\ error\ is\ returned.\ If\ the\ types\ are\ the\ same,\ no\ conversion\ is\ done.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01557}01557\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/even\ though\ some\ conversions\ aren't\ supported,\ LodePNG\ supports\ loading\ PNGs\ from\ any}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01558}01558\ \textcolor{comment}{\ colortype\ and\ saving\ PNGs\ to\ any\ colortype,\ sometimes\ it\ just\ requires\ preparing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01559}01559\ \textcolor{comment}{\ the\ raw\ image\ correctly\ before\ encoding.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01560}01560\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/both\ encoder\ and\ decoder\ use\ the\ same\ color\ converter.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01561}01561\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01562}01562\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ function\ lodepng\_convert\ does\ the\ color\ conversion.\ It\ is\ available\ in\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01563}01563\ \textcolor{comment}{interface\ but\ normally\ isn't\ needed\ since\ the\ encoder\ and\ decoder\ already\ call}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01564}01564\ \textcolor{comment}{it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01565}01565\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01566}01566\ \textcolor{comment}{Non\ supported\ color\ conversions:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01567}01567\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/color\ to\ grayscale\ when\ non-\/gray\ pixels\ are\ present:\ no\ error\ is\ thrown,\ but}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01568}01568\ \textcolor{comment}{the\ result\ will\ look\ ugly\ because\ only\ the\ red\ channel\ is\ taken\ (it\ assumes\ all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01569}01569\ \textcolor{comment}{three\ channels\ are\ the\ same\ in\ this\ case\ so\ ignores\ green\ and\ blue).\ The\ reason}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01570}01570\ \textcolor{comment}{no\ error\ is\ given\ is\ to\ allow\ converting\ from\ three-\/channel\ grayscale\ images\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01571}01571\ \textcolor{comment}{one-\/channel\ even\ if\ there\ are\ numerical\ imprecisions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01572}01572\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/anything\ to\ palette\ when\ the\ palette\ does\ not\ have\ an\ exact\ match\ for\ a\ from-\/color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01573}01573\ \textcolor{comment}{in\ it:\ in\ this\ case\ an\ error\ is\ thrown}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01574}01574\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01575}01575\ \textcolor{comment}{Supported\ color\ conversions:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01576}01576\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/anything\ to\ 8-\/bit\ RGB,\ 8-\/bit\ RGBA,\ 16-\/bit\ RGB,\ 16-\/bit\ RGBA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01577}01577\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/any\ gray\ or\ gray+alpha,\ to\ gray\ or\ gray+alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01578}01578\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/anything\ to\ a\ palette,\ as\ long\ as\ the\ palette\ has\ the\ requested\ colors\ in\ it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01579}01579\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/removing\ alpha\ channel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01580}01580\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/higher\ to\ smaller\ bitdepth,\ and\ vice\ versa}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01581}01581\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01582}01582\ \textcolor{comment}{If\ you\ want\ no\ color\ conversion\ to\ be\ done\ (e.g.\ for\ speed\ or\ control):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01583}01583\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/In\ the\ encoder,\ you\ can\ make\ it\ save\ a\ PNG\ with\ any\ color\ type\ by\ giving\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01584}01584\ \textcolor{comment}{raw\ color\ mode\ and\ LodePNGInfo\ the\ same\ color\ mode,\ and\ setting\ auto\_convert\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01585}01585\ \textcolor{comment}{false.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01586}01586\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/In\ the\ decoder,\ you\ can\ make\ it\ store\ the\ pixel\ data\ in\ the\ same\ color\ type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01587}01587\ \textcolor{comment}{as\ the\ PNG\ has,\ by\ setting\ the\ color\_convert\ setting\ to\ false.\ Settings\ in}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01589}01589\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01590}01590\ \textcolor{comment}{6.3.\ padding\ bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01591}01591\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01593}01593\ \textcolor{comment}{In\ the\ PNG\ file\ format,\ if\ a\ less\ than\ 8-\/bit\ per\ pixel\ color\ type\ is\ used\ and\ the\ scanlines}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01594}01594\ \textcolor{comment}{have\ a\ bit\ amount\ that\ isn't\ a\ multiple\ of\ 8,\ then\ padding\ bits\ are\ used\ so\ that\ each}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01595}01595\ \textcolor{comment}{scanline\ starts\ at\ a\ fresh\ byte.\ But\ that\ is\ NOT\ true\ for\ the\ LodePNG\ raw\ input\ and\ output.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01596}01596\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ raw\ input\ image\ you\ give\ to\ the\ encoder,\ and\ the\ raw\ output\ image\ you\ get\ from\ the\ decoder}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01597}01597\ \textcolor{comment}{will\ NOT\ have\ these\ padding\ bits,\ e.g.\ in\ the\ case\ of\ a\ 1-\/bit\ image\ with\ a\ width}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01598}01598\ \textcolor{comment}{of\ 7\ pixels,\ the\ first\ pixel\ of\ the\ second\ scanline\ will\ the\ 8th\ bit\ of\ the\ first\ byte,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01599}01599\ \textcolor{comment}{not\ the\ first\ bit\ of\ a\ new\ byte.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01600}01600\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01601}01601\ \textcolor{comment}{6.4.\ A\ note\ about\ 16-\/bits\ per\ channel\ and\ endianness}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01602}01602\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01604}01604\ \textcolor{comment}{LodePNG\ uses\ unsigned\ char\ arrays\ for\ 16-\/bit\ per\ channel\ colors\ too,\ just\ like}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01605}01605\ \textcolor{comment}{for\ any\ other\ color\ format.\ The\ 16-\/bit\ values\ are\ stored\ in\ big\ endian\ (most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01606}01606\ \textcolor{comment}{significant\ byte\ first)\ in\ these\ arrays.\ This\ is\ the\ opposite\ order\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01607}01607\ \textcolor{comment}{little\ endian\ used\ by\ x86\ CPU's.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01608}01608\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01609}01609\ \textcolor{comment}{LodePNG\ always\ uses\ big\ endian\ because\ the\ PNG\ file\ format\ does\ so\ internally.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01610}01610\ \textcolor{comment}{Conversions\ to\ other\ formats\ than\ PNG\ uses\ internally\ are\ not\ supported\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01611}01611\ \textcolor{comment}{LodePNG\ on\ purpose,\ there\ are\ myriads\ of\ formats,\ including\ endianness\ of\ 16-\/bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01612}01612\ \textcolor{comment}{colors,\ the\ order\ in\ which\ you\ store\ R,\ G,\ B\ and\ A,\ and\ so\ on.\ Supporting\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01613}01613\ \textcolor{comment}{converting\ to/from\ all\ that\ is\ outside\ the\ scope\ of\ LodePNG.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01614}01614\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01615}01615\ \textcolor{comment}{This\ may\ mean\ that,\ depending\ on\ your\ use\ case,\ you\ may\ want\ to\ convert\ the\ big}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01616}01616\ \textcolor{comment}{endian\ output\ of\ LodePNG\ to\ little\ endian\ with\ a\ for\ loop.\ This\ is\ certainly\ not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01617}01617\ \textcolor{comment}{always\ needed,\ many\ applications\ and\ libraries\ support\ big\ endian\ 16-\/bit\ colors}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01618}01618\ \textcolor{comment}{anyway,\ but\ it\ means\ you\ cannot\ simply\ cast\ the\ unsigned\ char*\ buffer\ to\ an}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01619}01619\ \textcolor{comment}{unsigned\ short*\ buffer\ on\ x86\ CPUs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01620}01620\ \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01640}01640\ \textcolor{comment}{8.\ chunks\ and\ PNG\ editing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01641}01641\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01642}01642\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01643}01643\ \textcolor{comment}{If\ you\ want\ to\ add\ extra\ chunks\ to\ a\ PNG\ you\ encode,\ or\ use\ LodePNG\ for\ a\ PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01644}01644\ \textcolor{comment}{editor\ that\ should\ follow\ the\ rules\ about\ handling\ of\ unknown\ chunks,\ or\ if\ your}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01645}01645\ \textcolor{comment}{program\ is\ able\ to\ read\ other\ types\ of\ chunks\ than\ the\ ones\ handled\ by\ LodePNG,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01646}01646\ \textcolor{comment}{then\ that's\ possible\ with\ the\ chunk\ functions\ of\ LodePNG.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01647}01647\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01648}01648\ \textcolor{comment}{A\ PNG\ chunk\ has\ the\ following\ layout:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01649}01649\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01650}01650\ \textcolor{comment}{4\ bytes\ length}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01651}01651\ \textcolor{comment}{4\ bytes\ type\ name}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01652}01652\ \textcolor{comment}{length\ bytes\ data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01653}01653\ \textcolor{comment}{4\ bytes\ CRC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01654}01654\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01655}01655\ \textcolor{comment}{8.1.\ iterating\ through\ chunks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01656}01656\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01657}01657\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01658}01658\ \textcolor{comment}{If\ you\ have\ a\ buffer\ containing\ the\ PNG\ image\ data,\ then\ the\ first\ chunk\ (the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01659}01659\ \textcolor{comment}{IHDR\ chunk)\ starts\ at\ byte\ number\ 8\ of\ that\ buffer.\ The\ first\ 8\ bytes\ are\ the}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01718}01718\ \textcolor{comment}{the\ ones\ that\ come\ before\ the\ PLTE\ chunk,\ the\ ones\ that\ come\ between\ the\ PLTE}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01722}01722\ \textcolor{comment}{chunks,\ but\ does\ not\ force\ any\ other\ ordering\ rules.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01725}01725\ \textcolor{comment}{info\_png.unknown\_chunks\_data[1]\ is\ the\ chunks\ after\ PLTE,\ before\ IDAT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lodepng_8h_source_l01726}01726\ \textcolor{comment}{info\_png.unknown\_chunks\_data[2]\ is\ the\ chunks\ after\ IDAT}}
